阿文

import * as DynamicEntryPlugin from "webpack/lib/DynamicEntryPlugin"; import * as webpack from "webpack"; export function addWebpackEntry( compilation: webpack.compilation.Compilation, context, name: string, entry: string ): Promise<never> { return new Promise((resolve, reject) => { const dep = DynamicEntryPlugin.createDependency(entry, name); compilation.addEntry(context, dep, name, err => { if (err) return reject(err); resolve(); }); }); }
